        <script>
function mainNavOpen(onoff) {
	if (onoff == 'on-sports') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-sports' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-schedules') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-schedules' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-gameday') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-gameday' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-tickets') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-tickets' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-fanzone') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-fanzone' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-giving') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-giving' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-athletics') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-athletics' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-recruits') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-recruits' }
	else if (onoff == 'on-links') { document.getElementById("nav").className = 'on-links' }
	else {
		document.getElementById("nav").className = ''
	}
}
function mainNavClose() { document.getElementById("nav").className = '' }
</script>

var utag_data;
function get_page_title() {
    if (document.querySelector(".StoryHeadline") !== null && document.querySelector(".StoryHeadline").innerHTML.length > 0) {
        return document.querySelector(".StoryHeadline").innerHTML;
    }

    var metas = document.getElementsByTagName('meta');
    for (i=0; i<metas.length; i++) {
        if (metas[i].getAttribute("property") == "og:title") {
            return metas[i].getAttribute("content");
        }
    }

    return document.title || '';
}
